bca_primary_district_update_zone_options_interloop = {
    optimize_memory

            }
            check_variable = {
                which = rank_zone_max
                value < value:bca_planet_setting_zone_rank_urban
            }
            OR = {
                    bca_primary_district_can_build_zone_urban = yes
                    bca_primary_district_can_build_zone_subterranean_urban = yes
                    bca_primary_district_can_build_zone_agrarian_anglers = yes

            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_option_map_wilderness_minerals_zone_minerals_wilderness
            add_variable = {
                which = zone_selector_options_count
                value = 1
            }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            NOR = {
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_wilderness_energy
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_selected_zone_type_$ZONE_SLOT$_wilderness_energy
            }
            check_variable = {
                which = rank_zone_max
                value = value:bca_planet_setting_zone_rank_wilderness_energy
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                bca_primary_district_can_build_zone_energy_wilderness = yes
            }
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_wilderness_energy
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_$SELECTOR_SLOT$_wilderness_energy
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_option_map_wilderness_energy_zone_energy_wilderness
            add_variable = {
                which = zone_selector_options_count
                value = 1
            }
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            NOR = {
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_wilderness_food
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_selected_zone_type_$ZONE_SLOT$_wilderness_food
            }
            check_variable = {
                which = rank_zone_max
                value = value:bca_planet_setting_zone_rank_wilderness_food
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                bca_primary_district_can_build_zone_food_wilderness = yes
            }
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_wilderness_food
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_$SELECTOR_SLOT$_wilderness_food
            set_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_option_map_wilderness_food_zone_food_wilderness
            add_variable = {
                which = zone_selector_options_count
                value = 1
            }
        }
    }
}

bca_secondary_district_update_zone_options_interloop = {
    optimize_memory


    set_variable = {
        which = rank_zone_max
        value = 0
    }
    # compare phase
    if = {
        limit = {
            NOR = {
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_option_elected_urban
                has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_selected_zone_type_$ZONE_SLOT$_urban
            }
            check_variable = {
                which = rank_zone_max
                value < value:bca_planet_setting_zone_rank_urban
            }
            # any zone of this typeset is available on the districts and can be built
            OR = {
                AND = {
                    bca_can_build_zone_urban = yes
                    OR = {
                    }
                }
                AND = {
                    bca_can_build_zone_subterranean_urban = yes
                    OR = {
                        has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_district_$ZONE_SLOT$_district_mining
                        has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_district_$ZONE_SLOT$_district_melting
                        has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_district_$ZONE_SLOT$_district_hollow_mountains
                    }
                }
                AND = {
                    bca_can_build_zone_agrarian_anglers = yes
                    OR = {
                        has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_zone_district_$ZONE_SLOT$_district_farming
